#USS Cole Attacks
country_event = {
	id = usa.2
	title = usa.2.t
	desc = usa.2.d
	picture = GFX_uss_cole_bombing
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		NOT = { has_start_date > 2016.1.1 }
	}

	#They Will be Missed
	option = {
		name = usa.2.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa.2.o1 executed"

		news_event = { hours = 6 id = usa_news.18 }
		add_named_threat = { threat = 0.5 name = usa.2.t }

		# Hate on SUD
		if = { limit = { country_exists = SUD }
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = SUD modifier = recent_actions_negative }
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = SUD modifier = recent_actions_negative }
		}
		else = {
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					has_government = fascism
					NOT = { tag = SAU }
					NOT = { tag = UAE }
					NOT = { tag = OMA }
					NOT = { tag = QAT }
					NOT = { tag = BHR }
					NOT = { tag = KUW }
					NOT = { tag = JOR }
				}
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = recent_actions_negative }
				reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = recent_actions_negative }
			}
		}
		USA_congress_small_opposition = yes
		set_country_flag = usa_uss_cole_attack

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}

	#Demand Sudan Repay!
	option = {
		name = usa.2.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa.2.o2 executed"

		news_event = { hours = 6 id = usa_news.18 }
		navy_experience = 5
		add_named_threat = { threat = 0.5 name = usa.2.t }

		#  Demand Repayment!
		if = { limit = { country_exists = SUD }
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = SUD modifier = recent_actions_negative }
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = SUD modifier = recent_actions_negative }
			SUD = { country_event = { id = usa.2000 days = 7 random_hours = 2 } }
		}
		else = {
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					has_government = fascism
					NOT = { tag = SAU }
					NOT = { tag = UAE }
					NOT = { tag = OMA }
					NOT = { tag = QAT }
					NOT = { tag = BHR }
					NOT = { tag = KUW }
					NOT = { tag = JOR }
				}
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = recent_actions_negative }
				reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = recent_actions_negative }
				country_event = { id = usa.2000 days = 7 random_hours = 2 }
			}
		}
		USA_congress_small_opposition = yes
		set_country_flag = usa_uss_cole_attack

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 0.25
				is_historical_focus_on = no
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 0.25
				has_government = nationalist
				has_government = communism
			}
		}
	}
}

#Sudan - America Demands Repayment for the USS Cole Bombing
country_event = {
	id = usa.2000
	title = usa.2000.t
	desc = usa.2000.d
	picture = GFX_uss_cole_bombing
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		USA = { has_country_flag = usa_uss_cole_attack }
		NOT = { has_start_date > 2016.1.1 }
	}

	option = { #Accept
		name = usa.2000.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa.2000.o1 executed"
		effect_tooltip = {
			set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -0.25 }
			modify_treasury_effect = yes
			USA = {
				set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 0.25 }
				modify_treasury_effect = yes
			}
		}

		#Response sent to America
		USA = { country_event = { id = usa.2001 days = 1 } }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}

	option = { #Refuse
		name = usa.2000.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa.2000.o2 executed"
		add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = 0.02 }
		recalculate_party = yes

		USA = { country_event = { id = usa.2002 days = 1 } }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}

#Microsoft acquires Visio
country_event = {
	id = usa.4
	title = usa.4.t
	desc = usa.4.d
	picture = GFX_stock_market
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_government = communism }
			NOT = { has_government = nationalist }
			NOT = {	is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 } }
			NOT = {	is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 } }
			NOT = {	is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 } }
			NOt = {	is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 } }
		}
		NOT = { has_start_date > 2016.1.1 }
	}

	#Allow the Acqusition
	option = {
		name = usa.4.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa.4.o1 executed"
		add_stability = -0.04
		811 = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}

		set_country_flag = USA_allowed_microsoft_merger
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 16 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.02 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.02 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { modify_economic_regulation = -4 }
		USA_modify_economic_regulation = yes
		set_temp_variable = { modify_wall_street = 3 }
		USA_modify_strength_of_wall_street = yes

		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = 3 }
		change_wall_street_opinion = yes
		change_small_medium_business_owners_opinion = yes
		change_industrial_conglomerates_opinion = yes

		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = usa.5 days = 25 random_hours = 10 } }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				has_global_flag = USA_STATUS_QUO_PATH
				add = 1
			}
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = no
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}

	#Stop the Merger!
	option = {
		name = usa.4.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa.4.o2 executed"
		add_stability = 0.02
		811 = { add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2 }
		set_country_flag = USA_stopped_microsoft_merger
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 4 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.02 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.02 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { modify_economic_regulation = 4 }
		USA_modify_economic_regulation = yes
		set_temp_variable = { modify_wall_street = -2 }
		USA_modify_strength_of_wall_street = yes

		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = -5 }
		change_wall_street_opinion = yes
		change_small_medium_business_owners_opinion = yes
		change_industrial_conglomerates_opinion = yes

		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = usa.5 days = 25 random_hours = 10 } }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = no
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				has_global_flag = USA_POLITICAL_REVOULUTION_PATH
				add = 2
			}
		}
	}
}

#America Online merges with Time Warner
country_event = {
	id = usa.5
	title = usa.5.t
	desc = usa.5.d
	picture = GFX_stock_market
	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		NOT = {
			has_government = communism
			has_government = nationalist
			is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
			is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
			is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 }
			is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 }
		}
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = USA_stopped_microsoft_merger
			has_country_flag = USA_allowed_microsoft_merger
		}
		date > 2000.2.1
		date < 2016.01.01
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Excellent!
	option = {
		name = usa.5.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa.5.o1 executed"
		add_political_power = -50
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 16 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.02 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.01 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { modify_economic_regulation = -2 }
		USA_modify_economic_regulation = yes

		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = 2 }
		change_wall_street_opinion = yes
		change_small_medium_business_owners_opinion = yes
		change_industrial_conglomerates_opinion = yes

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1.5
			modifier = {
				has_global_flag = USA_STATUS_QUO_PATH
				add = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				add = 0.75
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.10
				is_historical_focus_on = no
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 0.50
				has_country_flag = USA_allowed_microsoft_merger
			}
		}
	}

	#This is Illegal!
	option = {
		name = usa.5.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa.5.o2 executed"
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 4 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.05 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.02 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { modify_economic_regulation = 3 }
		USA_modify_economic_regulation = yes

		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = -3 }
		change_wall_street_opinion = yes
		change_small_medium_business_owners_opinion = yes
		change_industrial_conglomerates_opinion = yes

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0.50
			modifier = {
				has_global_flag = USA_POLITICAL_REVOULUTION_PATH
				add = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				add = 0.30
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.50
				is_historical_focus_on = no
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 0.75
				has_country_flag = USA_stopped_microsoft_merger
			}
		}
	}
}

#Elian Gonzalez Affair
country_event = {
	id = usa.7
	title = usa.7.t
	desc = usa.7.d
	picture = GFX_elian_gonzalez
	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		NOT = { has_government = communism }
		CUB = {
			has_government = communism
			exists = yes
		}
		NOT = { has_start_date > 2016.1.1 }
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {	#Send the boy back
		name = usa.7.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa.7.o1 executed"
		add_political_power = 50
		CUB = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = recent_actions_positive }
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = recent_actions_positive }
		}

		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = -3 }
		change_communist_cadres_opinion = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				80 = {
					country_event = { id = usa.22 days = 112 random_hours = 15 }
				}
				20 = {
					country_event = { id = usa.23 days = 112 random_hours = 15 }
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = usa.7.o1_tt

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				add = 3
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.50
			}
			modifier = {
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 } #Republican
				add = 0.25
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Keep him here
		name = usa.7.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa.7.o2 executed"
		add_stability = 0.01
		CUB = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = recent_actions_negative }
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = recent_actions_negative }
		}

		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 2 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.02 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.01 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 4 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.02 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.02 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = 5 }
		change_communist_cadres_opinion = yes

		add_named_threat = { threat = 5.0 name = usa.7.t }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				is_historical_focus_on = no
			}
		}
	}
}

#Greeneville sinks Ehime-Maru
country_event = {
	id = usa.8
	title = usa.8.t
	desc = usa.8.d
	picture = GFX_ehimemaru
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		NOT = { has_start_date > 2016.1.1 }
	}

	option = {	#Apologize
		name = usa.8.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa.8.o1 executed"
		add_stability = -0.01
		set_temp_variable = { arg_popularity = -0.01 }
		add_ruling_outlook_popularity = yes
		JAP = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = recent_actions_positive }
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = recent_actions_positive }
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				add = 0.25
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 0.10
				has_government = democratic
				has_government = neutrality
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#It's their fault
		name = usa.8.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa.8.o2 executed"
		add_named_threat = { threat = 0.5 name = usa.8.t }
		set_temp_variable = { arg_popularity = -0.02 }
		add_ruling_outlook_popularity = yes
		JAP = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = recent_actions_negative }
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = recent_actions_negative }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 20 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.03 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.03 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				has_government = communism
				has_government = nationalist
				add = 0.50
			}
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = no
				add = 0.25
			}
		}
	}
}

#Shooting of Kayla Rolland
country_event = {
	id = usa.11
	title = usa.11.t
	desc = usa.11.d
	picture = GFX_handgun
	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		has_full_control_of_state = 777 #Michigan
		date > 2000.1.1
		date < 2001.1.1
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #An Era of Gun Violence?
		name = usa.11.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa.11.o1 executed"
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.01
		set_temp_variable = { arg_popularity = -0.02 }
		add_ruling_outlook_popularity = yes
		set_country_flag = usa_era_of_gun_violence #Used for future USA Gun Events
		set_variable = { USA_frequency_percentage_for_gun_violence = 0.9 }
		set_variable = { USA_casualties_percentage_for_gun_violence = 0.95 }
	}
}

#2000 Phillips Explosion
country_event = {
	id = usa.12
	title = usa.12.t
	desc = usa.12.d
	picture = GFX_burning_oil_refinery
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		has_full_control_of_state = 800	#Texas
		date > 2000.03.20
		date < 2000.04.1
	}

	option = { #Accidents Happen
		name = usa.12.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa.12.o1 executed"
		add_stability = -0.04
		USA_congress_medium_opposition = yes

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 14 }
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 }
				add = 2
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Launch a Complete Investigation
		name = usa.12.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa.12.o2 executed"
		add_political_power = -75
		add_stability = -0.02

		change_wall_street_opinion = yes

		ai_chance = {

			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 } #Conservatism
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 14 } #Libertarian
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 } #RWP
			}

				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 } #Liberalism
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 } #Social Democracy

			}
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = usa.1000
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = { tag = USA }
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event usa.1000 executed"
		random_list = {
			#Political Establishment Reinforced
			60 = {
				modifier = {
					congress_low_support_trigger = yes
					factor = 1.25
				}
				modifier = {
					has_idea = political_establishment
					factor = 5
				}
				country_event = { id = usa.21 days = 21 random_hours = 5 }
			}
			#Third Party Gains
			15 = {
				modifier = {
					NOT = { congress_low_support_trigger = yes }
					factor = 1.25
				}
				modifier = {
					has_stability > 0.40
					factor = 1.5
				}
				country_event = { id = usa.18 days = 20 random_hours = 5 }
			}
			#Rise of Leftism
			10 = {
				modifier = {
					has_stability > 0.40
					factor = 1.5
				}
				modifier = {
					check_variable = { party_pop_array^2 > 0.10 }
					check_variable = { party_pop_array^3 > 0.10 }
					factor = 1.25
				}
				modifier = {
					NOT = { congress_low_support_trigger = yes }
					factor = 1.25
				}
				country_event = { id = usa.17 days = 20 random_hours = 5 }
			}
			#Rise of Traditionalism
			8 = {
				modifier = {
					has_stability > 0.40
					factor = 1.5
				}
				modifier = {
					check_variable = { party_pop_array^1 > 0.10 }
					check_variable = { party_pop_array^14 > 0.10 }
					check_variable = { party_pop_array^20 > 0.10 }
					factor = 1.25
				}
				modifier = {
					NOT = { congress_low_support_trigger = yes }
					factor = 1.25
				}
				country_event = { id = usa.19 days = 20 random_hours = 5 }
			}
			#Anti-Globalization Protests
			7 = {
				modifier = {
					has_government = nationalist
					factor = 1.25
				}
				country_event = { id = usa.20 days = 20 random_hours = 5 }
			}
		}
	}
}

		}

				add = -100
			}
		}

		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				is_in_faction = yes
				add = 50
			}
		}
	}

#Microsoft allowed to expand further
country_event = {
	id = usa.33
	title = usa.33.t
	desc = usa.33.d
	picture = GFX_court
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = USA
	}

	#Increased Economic Prosperity
	option = {
		name = usa.33.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa.33.o1 executed"
		increase_economic_growth = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				811 = {
					free_building_slots = {
						building = industrial_complex
						size > 1
						include_locked = yes
					}
				}
			}
			811 = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				811 = {
					free_building_slots = {
						building = industrial_complex
						size = 0
					}
				}
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = 7 }
		change_wall_street_opinion = yes
		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = 5 }
		change_industrial_conglomerates_opinion = yes
		change_small_medium_business_owners_opinion = yes

		set_country_flag = USA_allowed_microsoft_monopoly
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

	#Send in the Feds
	option = {
		name = usa.38.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa.38.o1 executed"
		add_political_power = -50
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -0.40 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes

		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = -3 }
		change_fossil_fuel_industry_opinion = yes
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}

	#The local authorities are capable
	option = {
		name = usa.38.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa.38.o2 executed"
		add_stability = -0.01
		set_temp_variable = { arg_popularity = -0.025 }
		add_ruling_outlook_popularity = yes

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}

		set_country_flag = USA_death_of_gus_hall
	}
	title = usa.60.t
	desc = usa.60.d
	picture = GFX_fathers_of_communism
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

		tag = USA
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_death_of_gus_hall }
		date > 2000.10.01
		date < 2001.10.31
	}

	option = {
		name = usa.60.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa.60.o1 executed"
		add_stability = 0.02

		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}

	option = {
		name = usa.60.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa.60.o2 executed"
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.01
		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = 3 }
		change_communist_cadres_opinion = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
					is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 4 }
				}
			}
			add_country_leader_trait = communist_sympathizer
		}
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 4 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.05 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.02 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_government = communism }
				country_event = { id = usa.63 days = 1000 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}

##Renogitate NAFTA
country_event = {
	id = usa.90
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	title = usa.90.t
	desc = usa.90.d
	picture = GFX_USA_generic

	#American-Benefited Deal
	option = {
		name = usa.90.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event usa.90.a"

		add_ideas = USA_pro_american_deal_idea

		effect_tooltip = {
			MEX = { add_ideas = USA_pro_american_deal_mex_can_idea }
			CAN = { add_ideas = USA_pro_american_deal_mex_can_idea }
		}
		clr_country_flag = USA_renogitate_nafta_flag
		set_country_flag = USA_pro_american_deal


		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = 5 }
		change_wall_street_opinion = yes
		change_small_medium_business_owners_opinion = yes
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0.5
			modifier = {
				add = 0.5
				has_government = nationalist
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 0.25
				has_government = communism
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 0.25
				is_historical_focus_on = no
			}
		}
	}

	#Mutually Beneficial Deal
	option = {
		name = usa.90.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event usa.90.b"

		add_ideas = USA_mutually_benefical_idea
		effect_tooltip = {
			MEX = { add_ideas = USA_mutually_benefical_idea }
			CAN = { add_ideas = USA_mutually_benefical_idea }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = 5 }
		change_wall_street_opinion = yes
		change_small_medium_business_owners_opinion = yes
		clr_country_flag = USA_renogitate_nafta_flag
		set_country_flag = USA_mutually_benefical_deal
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				add = 0.5
				has_government = democratic
			}
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				add = 3
			}
		}
	}

	#America First!
	option = {
		name = usa.90.c
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event usa.90.c"
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_leader = { name = "Donald Trump" ruling_only = yes }
				has_government = nationalist
			}
		}

		add_ideas = USA_pro_american_deal_idea
		effect_tooltip = {
			MEX = { add_ideas = USA_america_fist_deal_mex_can_idea }
			CAN = { add_ideas = USA_america_fist_deal_mex_can_idea }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = 5 }
		change_wall_street_opinion = yes
		change_small_medium_business_owners_opinion = yes
		clr_country_flag = USA_renogitate_nafta_flag
		set_country_flag = USA_american_first_deal

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				OR = {
					has_country_leader = { name = "Donald Trump" ruling_only = yes }
					has_government = nationalist
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Accept the Negotiated Deal
country_event = {
	id = usa.91
	title = {
		text = usa.91.t1
		trigger = {
			USA = { has_country_flag = USA_pro_american_deal }
		}
	}
	title = {
		text = usa.91.t2
		trigger = {
			USA = { has_country_flag = USA_mutually_benefical_deal }
		}
	}
	title = {
		text = usa.91.t3
		trigger = {
			USA = { has_country_flag = USA_american_first_deal }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = usa.91.d1
		trigger = {
			USA = { has_country_flag = USA_pro_american_deal }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = usa.91.d2
		trigger = {
			USA = { has_country_flag = USA_mutually_benefical_deal }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = usa.91.d3
		trigger = {
			USA = { has_country_flag = USA_american_first_deal }
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_politics_speak
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = MEX
			tag = CAN
		}
	}

	#Accept [USA.GetLeader] Terms
	option = {
		name = usa.91.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event usa.91.a"
		if = {
			limit = {
				USA = { has_country_flag = USA_pro_american_deal }
			}
			add_ideas = USA_pro_american_deal_mex_can_idea
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				USA = { has_country_flag = USA_mutually_benefical_deal }
			}
			add_ideas = USA_mutually_benefical_idea
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				USA = { has_country_flag = USA_american_first_deal }
			}
			add_ideas = USA_america_fist_deal_mex_can_idea
		}
		USA = { country_event = { id = diplomatic_response.1 days = 1 } }

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					USA = { has_country_flag = USA_pro_american_deal }
					USA = { has_country_flag = USA_american_first_deal }
				}
				factor = 0.50
			}
			modifier = {
				USA = { has_country_flag = USA_mutually_benefical_deal }
				add = 0.50
			}
		}
	}

	#Pull out of Nafta
	option = {
		name = usa.91.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event usa.91.b"
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					USA = { has_country_flag = USA_pro_american_deal }
					has_idea = USA_pro_american_deal_mex_can_idea
				}
			}
			remove_ideas = USA_pro_american_deal_mex_can_idea
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					USA = { has_country_flag = USA_mutually_benefical_deal }
					has_idea = USA_mutually_benefical_idea
				}
			}
			remove_ideas = USA_mutually_benefical_idea
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					USA = { has_country_flag = USA_american_first_deal }
					has_idea = USA_america_fist_deal_mex_can_idea
				}
			}
			remove_ideas = USA_america_fist_deal_mex_can_idea
		}
		remove_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = large_commercial_relations }
		USA = { country_event = { id = diplomatic_response.2 days = 1 } }

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				USA = { has_country_flag = USA_mutually_benefical_deal }
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					USA = { has_country_flag = USA_pro_american_deal }
					USA = { has_country_flag = USA_american_first_deal }
				}
				factor = 1.75
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = usa_vanilla.50
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = { tag = USA }
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event usa_vanilla.50"
		random_list = {
			20 = {
				modifier = {
					not = { congress_medium_support_trigger = yes }
					factor = 1.25
				}
				modifier = {
					not = { congress_low_support_trigger = yes }
					factor = 2
				}
				country_event = { id = usa_vanilla.40 days = 15 random_hours = 6 } #small support
			}
			20 = {
				modifier = {
					check_variable = { var = senators_support value = quorum_high compare = greater_than_or_equals }
					factor = 3
				}
				country_event = { id = usa_vanilla.42 days = 20 random_hours = 6 } #small opposition
			}
			15 = {
				modifier = {
					not = { congress_medium_support_trigger = yes }
					factor = 1.25
				}
				modifier = {
					not = { congress_low_support_trigger = yes }
					factor = 2
				}
				country_event = { id = usa_vanilla.44 days = 20 random_hours = 10 } #medium support
			}
			15 = {
				modifier = {
					check_variable = { var = senators_support value = quorum_high compare = greater_than_or_equals }
					factor = 3
				}
				country_event = { id = usa_vanilla.46 days = 20 random_hours = 10 }  #medium opposition
			}
			30 = { #investment opportunity
				modifier = {
					has_country_flag = USA_congress_investment
					factor = 0
				}
				country_event = { id = usa_vanilla.60 days = 10 random_hours = 15 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# senator wants investment in their state - hidden dispatch event
country_event = {
	id = usa_vanilla.60
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event usa_vanilla.60" }
	trigger = { tag = USA }
	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = USA_congress_investment
		if = {
			limit = { has_event_target = USA_congress_investment_state }
			clear_global_event_target = USA_congress_investment_state
		}
		random_list = {
			25 = {
				modifier = {
					NOT = {
						any_owned_state = {
							is_core_of = ROOT
							is_controlled_by = ROOT
							free_building_slots = {
								building = industrial_complex
								size > 0
								include_locked = no
							}
						}
					}
					factor = 0
				}
				random_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
						is_controlled_by = ROOT
						free_building_slots = {
							building = industrial_complex
							size > 0
							include_locked = no
						}
					}

					save_global_event_target_as = USA_congress_investment_state
					state_event = { id = usa_vanilla.61 trigger_for = controller }
				}
			}
			25 = {
				modifier = {
					NOT = {
						any_owned_state = {
							is_core_of = ROOT
							is_controlled_by = ROOT
							free_building_slots = {
								building = arms_factory
								size > 0
								include_locked = no
							}
						}
					}
					factor = 0
				}
				random_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
						is_controlled_by = ROOT
						free_building_slots = {
							building = arms_factory
							size > 0
							include_locked = no
						}
					}
					save_global_event_target_as = USA_congress_investment_state
					state_event = { id = usa_vanilla.62 trigger_for = controller }
				}
			}
			25 = {
				modifier = {
					NOT = {
						any_owned_state = {
							is_core_of = ROOT
							is_controlled_by = ROOT
							is_coastal = yes
							free_building_slots = {
								building = dockyard
								size > 0
								include_locked = no
							}
						}
					}
					factor = 0
				}
				random_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
						is_controlled_by = ROOT
						free_building_slots = {
							building = dockyard
							size > 0
							include_locked = no
						}
					}
					save_global_event_target_as = USA_congress_investment_state
					state_event = { id = usa_vanilla.64 trigger_for = controller }
				}
			}
			25 = {
				modifier = {
					NOT = {
						any_owned_state = {
							is_core_of = ROOT
							free_building_slots = {
								building = infrastructure
								size > 0
								include_locked = no
							}
						}
					}
					factor = 0
				}
				random_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
						is_controlled_by = ROOT
						free_building_slots = {
							building = infrastructure
							size > 0
							include_locked = no
						}
					}
					save_global_event_target_as = USA_congress_investment_state
					state_event = { id = usa_vanilla.63 trigger_for = controller }
				}
			}

# senator wants investment in civilian factory
country_event = {
	id = usa_vanilla.61
	title = usa_vanilla.61.t
	desc = usa_vanilla.61.desc
	picture = GFX_generic_factory

	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = { tag = USA }


	option = {
		name = usa_vanilla.61.a #accept
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event usa_vanilla.61.a"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		unlock_decision_tooltip = { decision = USA_invest_in_state_factory show_effect_tooltip = yes }
		event_target:USA_congress_investment_state = {
			set_state_flag = USA_congress_build_factory
			set_variable = { factory_goal = industrial_complex_level }
			add_to_variable = { factory_goal = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = usa_vanilla.61.b #refuse
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event usa_vanilla.61.b"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		ROOT = { clr_country_flag = USA_congress_investment }
		clear_global_event_target = USA_congress_investment_state
	}
}

	desc = usa_news.18.d
	picture = GFX_cole_attack

	major = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = usa_news.18.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa_news.18.o1 executed"
		trigger = { original_tag = USA }
	}

	option = {
		name = usa_news.18.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa_news.18.o2 executed"
		trigger = {
			NOT = { original_tag = USA }
			NOT = { original_tag = NKO }
			NOT = { original_tag = SUD }
			NOT = { has_war_with = USA }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = usa_news.18.o3
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa_news.18.o3 executed"
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = NKO
				has_war_with = USA
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = usa_news.18.o4
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa_news.18.o4 executed"
		trigger = {
			original_tag = SUD
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			USA = {
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = SUD
					modifier = recent_actions_negative
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = USA_FOCUS.2
	title = USA_FOCUS.2.t
	desc = USA_FOCUS.2.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_american_troops
	trigger = {
		tag = USA
	}

	#Deploy - the E-Brigade
	option = {
		name = USA_FOCUS.2.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: USA_FOCUS.2.a executed"
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_template = "Armored Brigade"
					}
				}
				division_template = {
					name = "Armored Brigade"
					regiments = {
						armor_Bat = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						armor_Bat = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						Arm_Inf_Bat = { x = 0 y = 2 }
						Arm_Inf_Bat = { x = 0 y = 3 }
						SP_Arty_Bat = { x = 1 y = 0 }
						Arm_Inf_Bat = { x = 1 y = 1 }
						Mech_Inf_Bat = { x = 1 y = 2 }
					}

					support = {
						H_Engi_Comp = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						SP_Arty_Battery = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					}
				}
			}
			114 = {
				create_unit = {
					division = "division_template = \"Armored Brigade\" start_experience_factor = 0.3 start_equipment_factor = 0.50"
					owner = USA
					prioritize_location = 3544
					count = 1
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_deploy_e_brigade_tt
		news_event = { id = USA_FOCUS.1 days = 1 }
	}
}

#Cabinet picks - Secretary of State
country_event = {
	id = USA_Cabinet_picks.0
	title = USA_Cabinet_picks.0.t
	desc = USA_Cabinet_picks.0.d
	picture = GFX_trump_desk
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		country_event = { id = USA_Cabinet_picks.1 days = 17 }
	}

	#Pick Rex Tillerson, western +relations with Russia
	option = {
		name = USA_Cabinet_picks.0.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: USA_Cabinet_picks.0.a executed"
		add_country_leader_trait = USA_Rex_Tillerson
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = SOV modifier = USA_Tillerson_EFFECT }
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = SOV modifier = USA_Tillerson_EFFECT }

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 3
			modifier = {
				factor = 1
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}
	#Pick Giuliani + western
	option = {
		name = USA_Cabinet_picks.0.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: USA_Cabinet_picks.0.b executed"
		add_country_leader_trait = USA_Giuliani

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
	#Pick Romney + western - stability (swamp)
	option = {
		name = USA_Cabinet_picks.0.c
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: USA_Cabinet_picks.0.c executed"
		add_country_leader_trait = USA_Romney
		add_stability = -0.02
		add_political_power = 50

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
	#Pick Alex Jones + nationalism
	option = {
		name = USA_Cabinet_picks.0.e
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: USA_Cabinet_picks.0.e executed"
		add_country_leader_trait = USA_Alex_Jones
		add_popularity = { ideology = nationalist popularity = 0.02 }
		recalculate_party = yes

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 0.5

		name = USA_FOCUS.6.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: USA_FOCUS.6.a executed"
		ISR = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = USA_ISR_Jerusalem_Capital }
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				or = {
					has_idea = sunni
					has_idea = shia
				}
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = USA_Recognize_Jerusalem_Capital }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				news_event = { id = USA_FOCUS.7 days = 3 }
			}
			news_event = { id = Israel.1 days = 90 } #temp
		}
		add_political_power = 25
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
	}

	option = { #eh, maybe later
		name = USA_FOCUS.6.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: USA_FOCUS.6.b executed"
		ISR = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = USA_Not_Jerusalem_Capital }
		}
	}

}

##2000's Recession
country_event = {
	id = usa_economic_events.init
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event usa_economic_events.init" }
	hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		date > 2006.1.1
		has_start_date < 2016.01.01
		tag = USA
		NOT = { has_country_flag = collapsed_nation }
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 300
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.5
			check_variable = { USA_economic_regulation_var < 90 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			check_variable = { USA_economic_regulation_var > 90 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			check_variable = { USA_strength_of_wall_street_var < 25 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 3.5
			check_variable = { USA_strength_of_wall_street_var > 25 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_idea = wall_street
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.10
			date > 2009.1.01
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = usa_great_fiancial_crisis #Global Flag for other Content Designing
		country_event = { id = usa_economic_events.1 days = 10 random_hours = 5 }
	}
}

##The Lehman Brothers Collapse!
country_event = {
	id = usa_economic_events.1
	title = usa_economic_events.1.t
	desc = usa_economic_events.1.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_lehmanbrothers
	Trigger = {
		Tag = USA
		NOT = { has_country_flag = collapsed_nation }
	}

	#Oh no, nationalize it!
	option = {
		name = usa_economic_events.1.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event usa_economic_events.1.a"
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -90 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
		recession = yes
		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = -5 }
		change_wall_street_opinion = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = usa_economic_nationalize_tt

		set_country_flag = usa_nationalize_one
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = usa_economic_events.2 days = 40 random_hours = 30 }
			news_event = { id = usa_economic_events_news.1 days = 1 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					has_government = nationalist
					has_government = communism
				}
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				nationalist > 0.30
				add = 1
			}
		}
	}

	#Bailout the bank!
	option = {
		name = usa_economic_events.1.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event usa_economic_events.1.b"
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -60 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
		recession = yes
		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = 5 }
		change_wall_street_opinion = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = usa_economic_bailout_tt

		#Obama/Democrat Route to handling the crisis
		set_country_flag = usa_bailout_one
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = usa_economic_events.2 days = 40 random_hours = 30 }
			news_event = { id = usa_economic_events_news.1 days = 1 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					has_government = nationalist
					has_government = communism
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = no
				factor = 0.50
			}
			modifier = {
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				add = 5
			}
		}
	}

	#Let it take its course
	option = {
		name = usa_economic_events.1.c
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event usa_economic_events.1.c"
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 16 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.02 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.02 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes

		recession = yes
		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = -5 }
		change_wall_street_opinion = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = usa_economic_donothing_tt

		#Begins the Libertarian/Republican Method of a Laissez Faire Approach
		set_country_flag = usa_nothing_one
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = usa_economic_events_news.1 days = 1 }
			country_event = { id = usa_economic_events.2 days = 40 random_hours = 30 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					has_government = nationalist
					has_government = communism
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 14 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 2
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 16 }
			}
		}
	}
}

			country_event = { id = usa_economic_events.3 days = 40 random_hours = 30 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = no
				add = 0.25
			}

		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event usa_economic_events.5.a"
		add_political_power = 50
		if = { #Bailout and Nationalization - Nationalization is the most unstable. It is very unpredictable
			limit = {
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 5
					has_country_flag = usa_bailout_four
					has_country_flag = usa_bailout_three
					has_country_flag = usa_bailout_two
					has_country_flag = usa_bailout_one
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_four
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_three
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_two
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_one
					check_variable = { USA_strength_of_wall_street_var > 30 }
					check_variable = { USA_economic_regulation_var < 40 }
				}
			}
			add_ideas = USA_economic_crisis_light_idea
			add_political_power = 50
		}
		else_if = { #Bailout and Nationalization
			limit = {
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 5
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_four
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_three
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_two
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_one
					has_country_flag = usa_bailout_four
					has_country_flag = usa_bailout_three
					has_country_flag = usa_bailout_two
					has_country_flag = usa_bailout_one
					check_variable = { USA_strength_of_wall_street_var > 10 }
					check_variable = { USA_economic_regulation_var < 60 }
				}
			}
			add_ideas = USA_economic_crisis_medium_idea
			add_political_power = 100
			add_stability = -0.025
		}
		else_if = { #Nationalization and Noting Can Lead Here
			limit = {
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 5
					has_country_flag = usa_nothing_four
					has_country_flag = usa_nothing_three
					has_country_flag = usa_nothing_two
					has_country_flag = usa_nothing_one
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_four
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_three
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_two
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_one
					check_variable = { USA_strength_of_wall_street_var < 40 }
					check_variable = { USA_economic_regulation_var < 90 }
				}
			}
			add_ideas = USA_economic_crisis_severe_idea
			add_political_power = 150
			add_stability = -0.05
		}
		country_event = { id = usa_economic_events.30 days = 70 random_hours = 35 }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = no
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 } #conservatism
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 14 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 13 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 16 }
				}
				add = 0.30
			}
		}
	}

	#Assist the Families
	option = {
		name = usa_economic_events.5.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event usa_economic_events.5.b"
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -150 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
		add_stability = 0.03
		if = { #Bailout and Nationalization - Nationalization is the most unstable. It is very unpredictable
			limit = {
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 5
					has_country_flag = usa_bailout_four
					has_country_flag = usa_bailout_three
					has_country_flag = usa_bailout_two
					has_country_flag = usa_bailout_one
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_four
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_three
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_two
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_one
					check_variable = { USA_strength_of_wall_street_var > 30 }
					check_variable = { USA_economic_regulation_var < 40 }
				}
			}
			add_ideas = USA_economic_crisis_light_idea
			add_political_power = 50
		}
		else_if = { #Bailout and Nationalization
			limit = {
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 5
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_four
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_three
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_two
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_one
					has_country_flag = usa_bailout_four
					has_country_flag = usa_bailout_three
					has_country_flag = usa_bailout_two
					has_country_flag = usa_bailout_one
					check_variable = { USA_strength_of_wall_street_var > 10 }
					check_variable = { USA_economic_regulation_var < 60 }
				}
			}
			add_ideas = USA_economic_crisis_medium_idea
			add_political_power = 100
			add_stability = -0.025
		}
		else_if = { #Nationalization and Noting Can Lead Here
			limit = {
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 5
					has_country_flag = usa_nothing_four
					has_country_flag = usa_nothing_three
					has_country_flag = usa_nothing_two
					has_country_flag = usa_nothing_one
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_four
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_three
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_two
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_one
					check_variable = { USA_strength_of_wall_street_var < 40 }
					check_variable = { USA_economic_regulation_var < 90 }
				}
			}
			add_ideas = USA_economic_crisis_severe_idea
			add_political_power = 150
			add_stability = -0.05
		}

		country_event = { id = usa_economic_events.30 days = 70 random_hours = 35 }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = no
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 } #conservatism
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 14 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 13 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 16 }
				}
				factor = 0.40
			}
		}
	}
}

#Random Events Until Recession is Over
country_event = {
	id = usa_economic_events.30
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] event usa_economic_events.3"
		random_list = {
			##Military Industry Leave the USA
			5 = {
				country_event = { id = usa_economic_events.31 days = 100 random_hours = 35 }
			}
			##Civilian Factories Leave the USA
			30 = {
				country_event = { id = usa_economic_events.32 days = 100 random_hours = 35 }
			}
			##Company Collapse
			15 = {
				country_event = { id = usa_economic_events.33 days = 100 random_hours = 35 }
			}
			##Company Goes Bankrupt
			50 = {
				country_event = { id = usa_economic_events.34 days = 100 random_hours = 35 }
			}
		}
	}
	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		has_idea = USA_economic_crisis_light_idea
		has_idea = USA_economic_crisis_medium_idea
		has_idea = USA_economic_crisis_severe_idea
		NOT = { has_country_flag = usa_american_recession_occured }
	}
}

#Military Industry Leaves the USA
country_event = {
	id = usa_economic_events.31
	title = usa_economic_events.31.t
	desc = usa_economic_events.31.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_handgun
	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		OR = {
			has_idea = USA_economic_crisis_light_idea
			has_idea = USA_economic_crisis_medium_idea
			has_idea = USA_economic_crisis_severe_idea
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = usa_american_recession_occured }
	}
	#Oh no
	option = {
		name = usa_economic_events.31.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event usa_economic_events.31.a"
		set_temp_variable = { arg_popularity = -0.02 }
		add_ruling_outlook_popularity = yes
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			remove_building = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = 1
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			remove_building = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = 1
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = recession
				}
				country_event = { id = usa_economic_events.30 days = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_idea = recession }
				}
				country_event = { id = usa_economic_events.35 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

#End of the American Recession
country_event = {
	id = usa_economic_events.35
	title = usa_economic_events.35.t
	desc = usa_economic_events.35.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_banking_crisis
	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		has_global_flag = usa_great_fiancial_crisis
		OR = {
			has_idea = USA_economic_crisis_light_idea
			has_idea = USA_economic_crisis_medium_idea
			has_idea = USA_economic_crisis_severe_idea
		}
		OR = {
			has_idea = stable_growth
			has_idea = fast_growth
			has_idea = economic_boom
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = usa_american_recession_occured
			has_country_flag = USA_american_recession_over
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 5
		modifier = {
			factor = 25
			has_idea = USA_economic_crisis_severe_idea
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 20
			has_idea = USA_economic_crisis_medium_idea
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 15
			has_idea = USA_economic_crisis_light_idea
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1000
			OR = {
				has_idea = recession
				has_idea = depression
				has_idea = stagnation
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			OR = {
				has_idea = stable_growth
				has_idea = fast_growth
				has_idea = economic_boom
			}
		}
	}
	#Glorious!
	option = {
		name = usa_economic_events.35.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event usa_economic_events.35.a"
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_political_power = 100
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = USA_economic_crisis_light_idea }
			remove_ideas = USA_economic_crisis_light_idea
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = USA_economic_crisis_medium_idea }
			remove_ideas = USA_economic_crisis_medium_idea
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = USA_economic_crisis_severe_idea }
			remove_ideas = USA_economic_crisis_severe_idea
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_american_recession_over

		news_event = { id = usa_economic_events_news.6 days = 1 }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

#News - Lehman Brothers Collapse
news_event = {
	id = usa_economic_events_news.1
	title = usa_economic_events_news.1.t
	Trigger = {
		NOT = {
			USA = {
			has_country_flag = collapsed_nation
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = usa_economic_events_news.1.d1
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_one
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = usa_economic_events_news.1.d2
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = usa_bailout_one
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = usa_economic_events_news.1.d3
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = usa_nothing_one
		}
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_world_lehmanbrothers
	major = yes

	#Hecking Wall Street
	option = {
		name = usa_economic_events_news.1.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event usa_economic_events_news.1.a"
		trigger = {
			tag = USA
		}
	}
	#A Tragic Day
	option = {
		name = usa_economic_events_news.1.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event usa_economic_events_news.1.b"
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = USA
				tag = CHI
				tag = SOV
				is_in_faction_with = SOV
				is_in_faction_with = CHI
				has_government = fascism
			}
		}
	}
	#Pathetic

			OR = {

				tag = SOV

		}

country_event = {
	id = donald_trump.0
	title = donald_trump.0.t
	desc = donald_trump.0.d
	picture = GFX_USA_muslim_ban
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Keep the ban limited
		name = donald_trump.0.o1 #Iraq, Syria, Iran, Sudan, Libya, Yemen, Somalia
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: donald_trump.0.o1 executed"
		set_country_flag = original_travel_ban
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.01 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 20 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.01 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes

		custom_effect_tooltip = travel_ban_challenge_possibility_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				80 = { #Bad Effect
					country_event = { id = donald_trump.1 days = 2 }
					set_country_flag = challenged_travel_ban
				}
				20 = { #Good Effect
					country_event = { id = donald_trump.7 days = 5 }
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
	}
	option = { #Expand the ban to other countries around the globe
		name = donald_trump.0.o2 #Adds Venezuela, Chad, and North Korea
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: donald_trump.0.o2 executed"
		set_country_flag = expanded_travel_ban
		add_political_power = -10
		add_stability = -0.01
		custom_effect_tooltip = travel_ban_small_challenge_possibility_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				60 = { #Bad Effect
					country_event = { id = donald_trump.1 days = 12 }
					set_country_flag = challenged_travel_ban
				}
				40 = { #Good Effect
					country_event = { id = donald_trump.7 days = 15 }
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
	}
}

		}
	}

			has_country_flag = expanded_travel_ban
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_USA_Election_2020
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = donald_trump.1.o1 #Iraq, Syria, Iran, Libya, Yemen, Somalia, Chad, Venezuela, North Korea
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: donald_trump.1.o1 executed"
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = original_travel_ban
		}
		clr_country_flag = original_travel_ban
		set_country_flag = revised_travel_ban
		add_political_power = -15
		add_stability = -0.01
		custom_effect_tooltip = travel_ban_small_challenge_possibility_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				67 = { #Bad Effect
					country_event = { id = donald_trump.3 days = 10 }
				}
				33 = { #Good Effect
					country_event = { id = donald_trump.7 days = 15 }
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
	}
	option = { #Push the ban through!
		name = donald_trump.1.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: donald_trump.1.o2 executed"
		add_political_power = -10
		add_stability = -0.02
		custom_effect_tooltip = travel_ban_failure_possibility_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				80 = { #Bad Effect
					country_event = { id = donald_trump.3 days = 35 }
					set_country_flag = rejected_travel_ban

						add = -20
						has_country_flag = expanded_travel_ban
					}
				}

					country_event = { id = donald_trump.7 days = 28 }
					modifier = {
						add = 20
						has_country_flag = expanded_travel_ban
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
	}
	option = { #We can't afford to be entangled in legal battles
		name = donald_trump.1.o3
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: donald_trump.1.o3 executed"
		add_stability = 0.01
		custom_effect_tooltip = travel_ban_drop_tt
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
	}
}

#Travel Ban Succeeds
country_event = {
	id = donald_trump.7
	title = donald_trump.7.t
	desc = {
		text = donald_trump.7.d1
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = challenged_travel_ban
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = donald_trump.7.d2
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = challenged_travel_ban
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = rejected_travel_ban
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = donald_trump.7.d3
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = rejected_travel_ban
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = expanded_travel_ban
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_USA_Election_2020
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Huzzah!
		name = donald_trump.7.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: donald_trump.7.o1 executed"
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = challenged_travel_ban
				}
			}
			add_political_power = 100
			add_stability = 0.03
			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 1 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.01 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 20 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.01 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = 50
			add_stability = 0.01
			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 1 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.005 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 20 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.005 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = travel_ban_drop_tt
	}
}

#Profits from Mining Start Pouring in
country_event = {
	id = donald_trump.11
	title = donald_trump.11.t
	desc = donald_trump.11.d
	picture = GFX_asteroid_in_orbit
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Huzzah!
		name = donald_trump.11.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: donald_trump.11.o1 executed"
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 20 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.002 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		capital_scope = {
			add_resource = {
				type = tungsten
				amount = 1
			}
			add_resource = {
				type = steel
				amount = 2
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { global.asteroid_mineral_count = 100 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = asteroid_mining_mined_tt
		add_to_variable = { treasury = asteroid_mining_rate }
		custom_effect_tooltip = asteroid_mining_revenue_tt
		set_country_flag = asteroid_mining
		news_event = donald_trump_news.3
	}
}
#Profits from Asteroid Mining
country_event = {
	id = donald_trump.12
	title = donald_trump.12.t
	desc = donald_trump.12.d
	picture = GFX_asteroid_in_orbit

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Excellent!
		name = donald_trump.12.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: donald_trump.12.o1 executed"
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = global.asteroid_mineral_count
					value = asteroid_mining_rate
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = asteroid_mining_mined_tt
			add_to_variable = { treasury = asteroid_mining_rate }
			subtract_from_variable = { global.asteroid_mineral_count = asteroid_mining_rate }
			custom_effect_tooltip = asteroid_mining_revenue_tt
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = asteroid_mining_not_enough_tt
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_global_flag = asteroid_mining_start }
				}
				set_global_flag = asteroid_mining_start
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						num_of_factories > 40
					}
					country_event = { days = 20 id = donald_trump.13 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
#Potential for Asteroid Mining
country_event = {
	id = donald_trump.13
	title = donald_trump.13.t
	desc = donald_trump.13.d
	picture = GFX_asteroid_in_orbit
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Invest in Asteroid Mining
		name = donald_trump.13.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: donald_trump.13.o1 executed"
		add_political_power = -50
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -25 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
		add_to_variable = { asteroid_mining_rate = 1 }
		add_to_variable = { global.asteroid_mining_rate = 1 }
		capital_scope = {
			add_resource = {
				type = steel
				amount = 1
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = asteroid_mining_opportunity_tt
		set_country_flag = asteroid_mining
		set_global_flag = asteroid_mining
	}
	option = { #Too expensive and a waste of our time!
		name = donald_trump.13.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: donald_trump.13.o2 executed"
	}
}

#US Launches Asteroid Mining Initiative
news_event = {
	id = donald_trump_news.2
	title = donald_trump_news.2.t
	desc = donald_trump_news.2.d
	picture = GFX_news_trump_announcement

	major = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #Space!
		trigger = {
			original_tag = USA
		}
		name = donald_trump_news.2.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: donald_trump_news.2.o1 executed"
	}
	option = { #Maybe we could expand into this...
		trigger = {
			num_of_factories > 25
			NOT = { original_tag = USA }
		}
		name = donald_trump_news.2.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: donald_trump_news.2.o2 executed"
	}
	option = { #Interesting
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				num_of_factories > 25
				original_tag = USA

		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.02 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes

		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 14 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.02 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes

		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 16 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.02 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes

		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 17 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.02 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes

		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 18 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.02 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes

		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 20 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.02 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes

		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 21 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.02 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes

		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 22 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.02 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes

		set_country_flag = disable_cycle_costs
			if = { limit = { has_idea = economic_boom }
				swap_ideas = { remove_idea = economic_boom add_idea = fast_growth }
			}
			else_if = { limit = { has_idea = fast_growth }
				swap_ideas = { remove_idea = fast_growth add_idea = stable_growth }
			}
			else_if = { limit = { has_idea = stable_growth }
				swap_ideas = { remove_idea = stable_growth add_idea = stagnation }
			}
			else_if = { limit = { has_idea = stagnation }
				swap_ideas = { remove_idea = stagnation add_idea = recession }
			}
			else_if = { limit = { has_idea = recession }
				swap_ideas = { remove_idea = recession add_idea = depression }
			}
			else_if = { limit = { has_idea = depression }
				add_political_power = -100
				add_stability = -0.05
			}
		clr_country_flag = disable_cycle_costs
		ingame_update_setup = yes

	}
}

		name = econ_event.11.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: econ_event.11.o1 executed"
		add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = us_fiscal_and_econ_policy }
		add_to_variable = { fiscal_econ_tax_efficiency = -0.05 }
		add_dynamic_modifier = {
			modifier = USA_the_global_financial_crisis
			days = 730
		}
		set_variable = { global_financial_crisis_consumer_goods_var = 0.10 }
		set_variable = { global_financial_crisis_factory_output_var = -0.15 }
		set_variable = { global_financial_crisis_construction_speed_var = -0.50 }
		set_variable = { global_financial_crisis_weekly_stability_var = -0.001 }
		set_variable = { global_financial_crisis_war_support_var = -0.001 }

		custom_effect_tooltip = consumer_goods10_tooltip
		custom_effect_tooltip = factory_output_minus15_tooltip
		custom_effect_tooltip = construction_speed_minus50_tooltip
		custom_effect_tooltip = weekly_stability_minus010_tooltip
		custom_effect_tooltip = weekly_war_support_minus010_tooltip

		set_country_flag = disable_cycle_costs
		if = { limit = { has_idea = economic_boom }
			swap_ideas = { remove_idea = economic_boom add_idea = fast_growth }
		}
		else_if = { limit = { has_idea = fast_growth }
			swap_ideas = { remove_idea = fast_growth add_idea = stable_growth }
		}
		else_if = { limit = { has_idea = stable_growth }
			swap_ideas = { remove_idea = stable_growth add_idea = stagnation }
		}
		else_if = { limit = { has_idea = stagnation }
			swap_ideas = { remove_idea = stagnation add_idea = recession }
		}
		else_if = { limit = { has_idea = recession }
			swap_ideas = { remove_idea = recession add_idea = depression }
		}
		else_if = { limit = { has_idea = depression }
			add_political_power = -100
			add_stability = -0.05
		}
		clr_country_flag = disable_cycle_costs

		ingame_update_setup = yes
		767 = {
			remove_building = {
				type = offices
				level = 1
			}
		}
		769 = {
			remove_building = {
				type = offices
				level = 1
			}
		}
		770 = {
			remove_building = {
				type = offices
				level = 1

				level = 1
			}
		}
		773 = {
			remove_building = {
				type = offices
				level = 1
			}
		}
	}

	desc = unrest_event.1.d
	picture = GFX_political_activist
	major = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = USA
	}

	option = {
		name = unrest_event.1.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: unrest_event.1.o1 executed"
		add_political_power = -100

		unlock_decision_tooltip = USA_political_diversity_act

		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 16 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.1 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.01 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes

		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = public_ignored1
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				has_global_flag = USA_REFORMED_REPUBLIC_PATH
				factor = 1000
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = unrest_event.1.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: unrest_event.1.o2 executed"

		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 16 }

		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.01 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}

}

country_event = {
	id = foreign_event.1
	title = foreign_event.1.t
	desc = foreign_event.1.d
	picture = GFX_handgun
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		USA = { has_completed_focus = USA_focus_supplying_our_sierra_leone
		}
	}
	option = { #We Appreciate The Help
		name = foreign_event.1.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: foreign_event.1.o1 executed"
		USA = {
			country_event = {
				id = foreign_event.111
				days = 2
			}
		}
		SIE = {
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = infantry_weapons3
				amount = 1000
				Producer = USA
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = command_control_equipment2
				amount = 100
				Producer = USA
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = util_vehicle_3
				amount = 50
				Producer = USA
			}
			set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -2 }
			modify_treasury_effect = yes

			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 1 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.04 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.04 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
	}
	option = { #We Are Holding Just Fine
		name = foreign_event.1.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: foreign_event.1.o2 executed"
		USA = {
				country_event = {
					id = foreign_event.112
					days = 2
				}
			}
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_political_power = 50

			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 20 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.04 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.04 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		}
	}
}
